DocInfo/PatchNote079=- Recon - Laser Designator no longer grants -armor, it instead grants 5%/10%/15% increased ranged attack speed to the designated target.
DocInfo/PatchNote080=- Recon - Laser Designator reveal radius improved from 2 to 2/3/4, energy cost increased from 5 to 8.
DocInfo/PatchNote081=- Recon - Motion Sensor no longer reduces enemy armor, now provides a global +1.5/+3 vison and detection buff to the team (Does not stack).
DocInfo/PatchNote082=- Recon - Renamed Motion Sensor to Battlefield Radar to better reflect its current effect on the team.
DocInfo/PatchNote083=- Engineer's X1 Bot and Recon's Reaper Drone are now Heroic - and thus receive xp shared from the team (7 radius).
DocInfo/PatchNote084=- Additionally, X1 Bot and Reaper Drone no longer take full xp from their own kills, those are instead evenly split among nearby teammates.
DocInfo/PatchNote085=- Engineer - Adjusted the level progression of the X1 Bot so that it is initially easier to level up, but harder at later levels.
DocInfo/PatchNote086=- Forward Observer - Slightly increased Airstrike friendy fire radius (from 1.5 to 2) so that it is not completely idiot proof.
DocInfo/PatchNote087=
DocInfo/PatchNote088=<Gameplay Changes>
DocInfo/PatchNote089=- Increased the push priority on Guardian of the Beta so he can't be body blocked.
DocInfo/PatchNote090=- Hades now has a 50% chance to kill each mind controlled zombie when the fight starts instead of always killing all zombies.
DocInfo/PatchNote091=- Due to X1 Bot becoming Heroic, the "Summoned" attribute has been added to most player-made units and mind controlled units.
DocInfo/PatchNote092=- Sync Module now looks for units with the "Summoned" attribute for the 18% damage bonus.
DocInfo/PatchNote093=
DocInfo/PatchNote094=<Qol Changes>
DocInfo/PatchNote095=- Added more coloring for Monstrous and Atrocious Elite Mutation so it is easier to tell them from regular zombies.
DocInfo/PatchNote096=- Forward Observer's shell count display now properly updates for other players too.
DocInfo/PatchNote097=- Added tooltips that reflect weapon mod's influence on splash and reload. (Does not yet reflect talent or passive ability influences).
DocInfo/PatchNote098=- Concentrated Fire and Focus Fire cooldowns are made to match their buff durations to avoid any confusion.
DocInfo/PatchNote099=- Erebos Cinematic will no longer play for normal/nightmare games.
DocInfo/PatchNote100=- Engineer's X1 Bot will now properly grow in size when upgraded.
DocInfo/PatchNote101=- Replaced Engineer's Reinforce icon with a colored one that differs from Sync Module's icon.
